EXTRACTED TEXT:
偏远地区混合能源站的自主监测与维护 一座高原试验站依靠太阳能阵列、锂电池和小型柴油发电机供电。微电 网需要持续支持诊所、无线电中继、气象设备和安全照明。冬季道路可能 封闭数日，网络也不稳定，因此本地控制器每二百毫秒采集电压、电流、 温度与振动数据，并在能源不足时优先保障医疗和通信负载。完整记录保 存在站内，只有压缩后的状态摘要会在链路恢复时发送到控制中心。 二〇二五年十月十八日，一场沙尘风暴使太阳能输出在十五分钟内下降 百分之三十四电池柜温度升高八摄氏度，逆变器风扇还出现异常低频振 动。控制器没有关闭整座电站，而是断开非必要加热装置、降低部分照明 功率并启动备用发电机。诊断模块随后提出三个可能原因：太阳能板被碎 屑遮挡、风扇轴承磨损，以及电池连接器的接触电阻上升。 风暴减弱后，技术员用头戴式摄像设备读取铭牌、序列号和报警代码. 本地处理单元再与离线维护手册进行比对。由于资料涉及关键基础设施 图像没有上传云端。采集程序先确认整个标签位于安全边界内，并分别检 查全图和上部区域的清晰度：若画面被裁切，耳机会提示向左、向右或向 后移动。目标只有连续四帧稳定且文字足够清楚时才会保存。第二天的日 志表明，自动排序与人工判断一致：先清理面板，再更换风扇轴承，最后 紧固电池端子。处置用了六分钟，关键服务未中断。这说明可靠的自动化 必须解释判断、承认不确定性，并把最终决定留给人。
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TRANSLATED TEXT:
Autonomous monitoring and maintenance of hybrid power stations in remote areas A plateau test station relies on solar arrays, lithium batteries and a small diesel generator to power it. Micro-networks need to continue to support clinics, radio relay, weather equipment and safety lighting. Roads may be closed for days in winter and the network is unstable, so local controllers collect voltage, current, temperature and vibration data every 200 milliseconds, and prioritize medical and communications loads when energy is scarce. Complete logs are stored on the station, and only compressed status summaries are sent to the control center when the link is restored. On October 18, 2005, a sandstorm caused solar output to drop in fifteen minutes. The temperature of the battery cabinet rose eight degrees Celsius by 34 percent, and the inverter fan also showed abnormally low frequency vibrations. Instead of shutting down the entire power plant, the controller disconnects unnecessary heating devices, lowers partial lighting, power and starts the backup generator. The diagnostic module then suggests three possible causes: solar panel breakage, aluminum shielding, fan bearing wear, and increased contact resistance of the battery connector. After the storm weakened, technicians used head-mounted cameras to read the insignia, serial numbers and alarm codes. The local processing unit was then compared with the offline maintenance manual. The images are not uploaded to the cloud because of critical infrastructure. The capture process first confirms that the entire label is within the safe boundary and checks the clarity of the whole image and the upper region separately: if the image is cropped, the earpiece is prompted to move left, right or backwards. The target is saved only when the sequence of four syllables is stable and the text is sufficiently clear. The next day's logs showed that the automatic sorting was consistent with the artificial judgment: first the panel was cleaned, then the fan bearings were replaced, and finally the battery terminals were tightened. The disposal took six minutes and critical services were not interrupted. This shows that reliable automation must interpret judgments, acknowledge uncertainty, and leave the final decision to humans.

TRANSLATED TEXT:
Technical manual of specifications Autonomous operation and integration of navigation systems of vehicles Unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) U 0 Other Chapter I: Systems engineering and integration specifications The of the cell 1.1 Aerodynamic configuration and analysis of structural integrity This Regulation lays down the technical design and installation standards for unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) systems operating in rural weather conditions. The design of the cell structure must have a precise balance of structural rigidity. The aerodynamic efficiency and vacuum mass ratio for fixed-wing drones using long-range ailerons. The design of the main tongeron must give priority to high-module carbon fibre fieldsite materials (other than class T700 or T800) This ensures adequate torsion resistance under extreme manoeuvre loads (+4 5G to 4.00) (02) The internal geomeotic topology of the cell must necessarily include the zoning of the ethecaramagnetic capacitance (ECM) High-frequency radio frequency transmitters (such as data station antennas and video transmission modules) must be physically isolated from high-precision analogue sensors (such as inereal IMU measurement units and barometers) The cell envelope must incorporate tension-conducting meshes or tinting paints in the critical tones in order to attenuate the electromagnetic trans-wire interference generated by the power cables of the peak current generators. All internal supports must adopt a topologically optimized design combining aeronautical grade aluminium alloys (7075-T6) or engineering plastics (PEEK) by means of an additive manufacturing process, thus minimising overall vacuum mass and ensuring the necessary mechanical strength. EXTRACTED TEXT:
Surveillance autonome d'une station énergétique isolée Sur un platesu difficile d'accès, une station alimente un dispensaire un relais radio des instruments météorologiques et l'eclairage de securté Le micro-reseau réunit des panneaux solaires, des batteries au lithium et un petit genérateur diesel Comme la route peut rester fermée plusieurs jours, un contrôleur mesure la tension. le courant la température et les vibrations toutes les 200 millisecondes Les données détaillées restent sur place seul un résumé compressé est transmis lorsque la liaison fonctionne Les équipements médicaux et de communication sont prioritaires Le 16 octobre 2025, une tempéte de poussière a réduit la production solaire de 34 % en quinze minutes La température de l'armoire de batteries a augmenté de 8 "C. tandis que le ventilateur de l'onduleur produisait une vibration anormale. Au lieu d'arrêter la station, le système a coupé le chauffage secondaire, réduit certains éclairages et démarré le groupe de secours Il a identifié trois causes possibles des débris sur les panneaux. un roulement usé et une résistance croissante dans un connecteur de batterie Après la tempéte, une caméra portée sur la téte a lu les plaques et les codes d'alarme. puis un processeur local les a comparés au manuel hors ligne Aucune image sensible n'a été envoyée dans le nuage. Le logiciel exigeait que l'étiquette entière reste dans une marge sure: il contrôlait aussi la netteté générale et celle de la partie supérieure Une consigne sonore demandait de reculer si un bord manquait, et quatre images stables étaient nécessaires. Les ingenieurs ont ensuite confirmé l'ordre proposé nettoyer les panneaux, remplacer le roulement. puis resserrer le connecteur L'intervention a duré six minutes sans interrompre un service critique Une automatisation fiable doit reconnaltre l'incertitude et laisser la décision finale à l'opérateur.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TRANSLATED TEXT:
Self-monitoring of an isolated power station On a difficult-to-reach platform, a station feeds a dispensary, a radio relay for weather instruments and secure lighting. A micro-sprinkler contains solar panels, lithium batteries and a small diesel generator. Current temperature and vibrations every 200 milliseconds Detailed data remains in place Only a compressed summary is transmitted when the link is working Medical equipment and communication are priority On October 16th, 2025, a dust storm reduced solar output by 34% in fifteen minutes. The temperature of the battery cabinet rose by 8 "C. While the inverter fan was producing an abnormal vibration. Instead of shutting down the station, the system turned off the secondary heating, reduced some of the lights, and started the rescue team. a worn bearing and increasing resistance in a battery connector After the storm, a head-mounted camera read the license plates and alarm codes. And then a local processor matched them to the offline manual. No sensitive images were sent to the cloud. The software required that the entire label remain within a safe margin, it also controlled the overall sharpness and the sharpness of the upper part. A sound command asked to back up if an edge was missing, and four stable frames were needed. The engineers then confirmed the proposed order to clean the panels, replace the bearing. Then tighten the connector The operation lasted six minutes without interrupting a critical service Reliable automation must acknowledge uncertainty and leave the final decision to the operator.

Monitoring of an isolated power station On a difficult-to-reach site, a slimming station, a medical clinic, a radio relay, weather instruments and safety lighting. The micro-resus is composed of solar panels, lithium batteries and a small diesel generator As the road may remain closed for several days, a controller measures voltage, current temperature and vibrations every 200 milliseconds Detailed data remains on the plate, only a compressed summary is transmitted when the link is operational Medical equipment ef communication are priority On October 18th, 2025, a dust storm reduced solar output by 34% in fifteen minutes. While the inverter fan was producing an abnormal vibration instead of shutting down the station. The system turned off the secondary heating, reduced some of the lights, and started the rescue group. He identified three possible causes of the debris on the panels, a worn bearing and increasing resistance in a battery connector. The software required the entire label to remain within a certain range, and it also controlled the overall sharpness and that of the upper part. A sound command asked to back up if an edge was missing and four stable frames were needed. The engineers then confirmed the proposed order: clean the panels, replace the bearing, then tighten the connector The operation lasted six minutes without interrupting a critical service Reliable automation must recognize uncertainty and leave the final decision to the operator

No sensitive images were sent to the cloud. The software required the entire label to remain within a certain range, and it also controlled the overall sharpness and that of the upper part. A sound command asked to back up if an edge was missing and four stable frames were needed. The engineers then confirmed the proposed order: clean the panels, replace the bearing, then tighten the connector The operation lasted six minutes without interrupting a critical service Reliable automation must recognize uncertainty and leave the final decision to the operator

EXTRACTED TEXT:
Surveillance autonome d'une station énergétique isolée Sur un plateau difficile d'accès, une station alimente un dispensaire un relais radio. des instruments metéorologiques et l'éclairage de sécurite Le micro-reseau reunit des panneaux solaires. des batteries au lithium et un petit genérateur diesel Comme la route peut rester fermée plusieurs jours. un contrôleur mesure la tension, le courant. la température et les vibrations toutes les 200 millisecondes Les données détaillées restent sur place, seul un résume compressé est transmis lorsque la liaison fonctionne Les équipements médicaux et de communication sont prioritaires. Le 18 octobre 2025, une tempête de poussière a réduit la production solaire de 34 % en quinze minutes La température de l'armoire de batteries a augmenté de 8 °C, tandis que le ventilateur de l'onduleur produisait une vibration anormale Au lieu d arrêter la station, le système a coupé le chauffage secondaire, réduit certains éclairages et démarré le groupe de secours Il a identifié trois causes possibles des débris sur les panneaux, un roulement usé et une résistance croissante dans un connecteur de batterie Après la tempête, une caméra portée sur la tête a lu les plaques et les codes d'alarme. puis un processeur local les a comparés au manuel hors ligne Aucune image sensible n'a été envoyée dans le nuage Le logiciel exigeait que l'étiquette entière reste dans une marge sure; il contrôlait aussi la netteté générale et celle de la partie supérieure Une consigne sonore demandait de reculer si un bord manquait, et quatre images stables étaient nécessaires Les ingénieurs ont ensuite confirmé l'ordre propose nettoyer les panneaux, remplacer le roulement, puis resserrer le connecteur L'intervention a duré six minutes sans interrompre un service critique Une automatisation fiable doit reconnaitre l'incertitude et laisser la décision finale à l'opérateur
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
TRANSLATED TEXT:
Self-monitoring of an isolated power station On a hard-to-reach shelf, a station feeds a medical clinic a radio relay. The micro irrigation system is a combination of solar panels. Lithium batteries and a small diesel generator as the road may remain closed for several days. A controller measures the voltage, the current. temperature and vibrations every 200 milliseconds Detailed data remains in place, only a compressed summary is transmitted when the link is operational Medical and communication equipment is a priority. On October 18, 2025, a dust storm reduced solar output by 34% in fifteen minutes The temperature of the battery cabinet rose by 8°C, while the inverter fan was producing an abnormal vibration Instead of shutting down the station, the system cut off the secondary heating, reduced some lights and started the rescue group He identified three possible causes of debris on the panels, a worn bearing and increasing resistance in a battery connector After the storm, a head-mounted camera read the license plates and alarm codes. Then a local processor compared them to the offline manual No sensitive image was sent to the cloud The software required that the entire tag remain in a safe margin; it also controlled the overall sharpness and that of the top part A sound command asked to back up if an edge was missing, and four stable images were needed The engineers then confirmed the order suggested cleaning the panels, replacing the bearing, then tightening the connector The intervention lasted six minutes without interrupting a critical service A reliable automation must recognize uncertainty and leave the final decision to the operator

Surveillance autonome d'une station énergétique isolée Sur un plateau difficile d accès une station alimente un dispensaire un retais radio des instruments météorologiques et l'éclairage de plusieurs jours. un contróleur mesure la tension. le courant la température et les vibrations toutes les 200 millisecondes Les données détaillées restent sur place. seul un résume compresse est transmis lorsque la liaison fonctionne Les equipements médicaux et de communication sont prioritaires Le 18 octobre 2025, une tempète de poussière a réduit la production solaire de 34 % en quinze minutes La température de l'armoire de batteries a augmenté de 8 C. tandis que le ventilateur de l'onduleur produisait une vibration anormale Au lieu d'arrêter la station le système a coupé le chauffage secondaire, réduit certains éclairages et démarré le groupe de secours Il a identifié trois causes possibles des débris sur les panneaux, un roulement usé et une résistance croissante dans un connecteur de balterie Après la tempête, une camèra portée sur la tête a lu les plaques et les codes d'alarme. puis un processeur local les a comparès au manuel hors ligne Aucune image sensible n'a été envoyée dans le nuage Le logiciel exigeait que l'étiquette entière reste dans une marge sure il contrôlait aussi la netteté gènérale et celle de la partie supérieure Une consigne sonore demandait de reculer si un bord manquait et quatre images stables étaient nécessaires Les ingénieurs ont ensuite confirmé l'ordre proposè nettoyer les panneaux, remplacer le roulement puis resserrer le connecteur L'intervention a durè six minutes sans interrompre un service critique Une automatisation fiable doit reconnaltre l'incertitude et laisser la décision finale à l'opérateur

TRANSLATED TEXT:
Self-monitoring of an isolated power station On a hard-to-reach plateau a station feeds a medical clinic a radio relay of weather instruments and lighting for several days. A controller measures the voltage. The current, the temperature and the vibrations every 200 milliseconds, the detailed data stays in place. Only a compressed summary is transmitted when the link is working Medical and communication equipment is a priority On 18 October 2025, a dust storm reduced solar output by 34% in 15 minutes The temperature of the battery cabinet rose by 8 C. Instead of shutting down the station, the system turned off the secondary heating, reduced some of the lights and started the rescue group. It identified three possible causes of the debris on the panels, a worn-out bearing and increasing resistance in a battery connector. Then a local processor compared them to the offline manual No sensitive image was sent to the cloud The software required that the entire tag remain in a safe margin It also controlled the overall sharpness and that of the top part A sound command asked to back up if an edge was missing and four stable images were needed The engineers then confirmed the proposed order Clean the panels, replace the bearing and then tighten the connector The intervention lasted six minutes without interrupting a critical service A reliable automation must reconstitute the uncertainty and leave the final decision to the operator

Surveillance autonome d'une station énergétique isolée Sur un plateau difficile d'accès, une station alimente un dispensaire. un relais radio, des instruments météorologiques et l'éclairage de sécurité Le micro-reseau reunit des panneaux solaires, des batteries au lithium et un petit genérateur diesel Comme la route peut rester fermée plusieurs jours. un contrôleur mesure la tension le courant la température et les vibrations toutes les 200 millisecondes Les données detaillees restent sur place, seul un résumé compresse est transmis lorsque la liaison fonctionne Les équipements médicaux et de communication sont prioritaires Le 18 octobre 2025. une tempête de poussière a réduit la production solaire de 34 % en quinze minutes La température de l'armoire de batteries a augmenté de 8 "C. tandis que le ventilateur de l'onduleur produisait une vibration anormale Au lieu d'arrèter la station, le système a coupe le chauffage secondaire, réduit certains éclairages et démarré le groupe de secours Il a identifié trois causes possibles des débris sur les panneaux, un roulement usé et une résistance croissante dans un connecteur de batterie Après la tempête une camèra portee sur la tête a lu les plagues et les codes d'alarme. puis un processeur local les a comparés au manuel hors ligne Aucune image sensible n'a eté envoyée dans le nuage Le logiciel exigeait que l'etiquette entière reste dans une marge süre, il contrôlait aussi la nettete générale et celle de la partie supérieure Une consigne sonore demandait de reculer si un bord manquait, et quatre images stables étalent necessaires. Les ingenieurs ont ensuite confirme l'ordre propose nettoyer les panneaux, remplacer le roulement, puis resserrer le connecteur. L'intervention a dure six minutes sans interrompre un service critique Une automatisation fiable doit reconnaitre lincertitude et laisser la décision finale a l'opérateur

TRANSLATED TEXT:
Self-monitoring of an isolated power station On a hard-to-reach shelf, a station feeds a dispensary. A radio relay, weather instruments and safety lighting The micro-sprinkler brings together solar panels, lithium batteries and a small diesel generator As the road may remain closed for several days. A controller measures voltage, current, temperature and vibration every 200 milliseconds Detailed data remains in place, only a concise summary is transmitted when the link is operational Medical equipment and communication are priority It's the 18th of October 2025. A dust storm reduced solar output by 34% in 15 minutes. Instead of shutting down the station, the system turned off the secondary heating, reduced some of the lights and started the backup unit. It identified three possible causes of debris on the panels, worn bearings and increasing resistance in a battery connector. After the storm, a head-mounted camera read out the pests and alarm codes. A local processor then compared them with the offline manual No sensitive image was sent to the cloud The software required the entire tag to remain within a timeframe, it also controlled the overall sharpness and that of the top part A sound command asked to back up if an edge was missing, and four stable frames were required. The engineers then confirmed the proposed order to clean the panels, replace the bearing, and then tighten the connector. The intervention lasts six minutes without interrupting a critical service A reliable automation must recognize certainty and leave the final decision to the operator
